ì¸ì½”ë”© ë¬¸ì œë¡œ ì¸í•´ ë°°ì¹˜ íŒŒì¼ì´ ê¹¨ì§„ ê²ƒ ê°™ìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤. ë‹¤ìŒì„ ìˆ˜ë™ìœ¼ë¡œ í•´ë³´ì„¸ìš”:

batch
@echo off
echo ========================================
echo Floor Plan Editor Server Start Script
echo ========================================
echo.

cd /d "%~dp0"

echo Current directory: %cd%
echo.

echo Checking Node.js installation...
node --version
if errorlevel 1 (
    echo.
    echo ERROR: Node.js is not installed!
    echo Please download and install Node.js from https://nodejs.org/
    echo.
    pause
    exit /b 1
)

echo.
echo Checking npm installation...
npm --version
if errorlevel 1 (
    echo.
    echo ERROR: npm is not installed!
    echo Please reinstall Node.js from https://nodejs.org/
    echo.
    pause
    exit /b 1
)

echo.

if not exist "node_modules\" (
    echo node_modules folder not found. Running npm install...
    echo.
    npm install
    if errorlevel 1 (
        echo.
        echo ERROR: npm install failed!
        echo Please check your internet connection and try again.
        echo.
        pause
        exit /b 1
    )
    echo.
    echo npm install complete!
    echo.
) else (
    echo node_modules already exists.
    echo.
)

echo Starting Floor Plan Editor Server...
echo.
echo Server will be available at http://localhost:3002
echo Editor interface at http://localhost:3002/editor
echo.
echo Press Ctrl+C to stop the server.
echo.

npm start

if errorlevel 1 (
    echo.
    echo ERROR: Server failed to start!
    echo.
    pause
)

pause

// App.jsx
import { FloorPlanProvider } from './context/FloorPlanContext';
import Header from './components/Layout/Header';
import FloorTabs from './components/Layout/FloorTabs';
import CanvasArea from './components/Canvas/CanvasArea';
import ModalsContainer from './components/Modals/ModalsContainer';

function App() {
  return (
    <FloorPlanProvider>
      <div className="h-screen flex flex-col bg-gray-50">
        <Header />
        <div className="flex-1 flex">
          <FloorTabs />
          <CanvasArea />
        </div>
        <ModalsContainer />
      </div>
    </FloorPlanProvider>
  );
}
2.2 Context API ì„¤ì •
jsx
// context/FloorPlanContext.jsx
import { createContext, useReducer, useContext } from 'react';

const FloorPlanContext = createContext();

const initialState = {
  rooms: [],
  selectedRoomIds: [],
  activeFloor: '1F',
  viewState: {
    zoom: 1,
    panX: 0,
    panY: 0
  },
  history: [],
  historyIndex: -1,
  modalState: {
    type: null,
    data: null
  }
};

function floorPlanReducer(state, action) {
  switch (action.type) {
    case 'ADD_ROOM':
      return { ...state, rooms: [...state.rooms, action.payload] };
    case 'UPDATE_ROOM':
      return {
        ...state,
        rooms: state.rooms.map(room =>
          room.id === action.payload.id ? { ...room, ...action.payload } : room
        )
      };
    case 'SET_SELECTED':
      return { ...state, selectedRoomIds: action.payload };
    case 'SET_VIEW_STATE':
      return { ...state, viewState: { ...state.viewState, ...action.payload } };
    // ... ë” ë§ì€ ì•¡ì…˜ë“¤
    default:
      return state;
  }
}

export function FloorPlanProvider({ children }) {
  const [state, dispatch] = useReducer(floorPlanReducer, initialState);
  
  return (
    <FloorPlanContext.Provider value={{ state, dispatch }}>
      {children}
    </FloorPlanContext.Provider>
  );
}

export const useFloorPlan = () => useContext(FloorPlanContext);
ğŸ“‹ Phase 3: Canvas ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ ë§ˆì´ê·¸ë ˆì´ì…˜
3.1 FloorCanvas ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸
jsx
// components/Canvas/FloorCanvas.jsx
import { useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useFloorPlan } from '../../context/FloorPlanContext';
import CanvasController from './CanvasController';

export default function FloorCanvas({ floor }) {
  const canvasRef = useRef(null);
  const controllerRef = useRef(null);
  const { state, dispatch } = useFloorPlan();
  
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!canvasRef.current) return;
    
    // Canvas Controller ì´ˆê¸°í™” (ê¸°ì¡´ canvasRenderer.js ë¡œì§ í™œìš©)
    controllerRef.current = new CanvasController(canvasRef.current, {
      onRoomSelect: (roomId) => dispatch({ type: 'SET_SELECTED', payload: [roomId] }),
      onRoomUpdate: (room) => dispatch({ type: 'UPDATE_ROOM', payload: room }),
      onViewChange: (viewState) => dispatch({ type: 'SET_VIEW_STATE', payload: viewState })
    });
    
    return () => controllerRef.current?.destroy();
  }, [dispatch]);
  
  // ìƒíƒœ ë³€ê²½ ì‹œ ë‹¤ì‹œ ë Œë”ë§
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!controllerRef.current) return;
    
    const roomsToRender = floor 
      ? state.rooms.filter(r => r.floor === floor)
      : state.rooms;
      
    controllerRef.current.render({
      rooms: roomsToRender,
      selectedIds: state.selectedRoomIds,
      viewState: state.viewState
    });
  }, [state.rooms, state.selectedRoomIds, state.viewState, floor]);
  
  return (
    <canvas 
      ref={canvasRef}
      className="w-full h-full cursor-grab active:cursor-grabbing"
    />
  );
}
ğŸ“‹ Phase 4: Custom Hooks ìƒì„±
4.1 useCanvas Hook
jsx
// hooks/useCanvas.js
import { useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
import { useFloorPlan } from '../context/FloorPlanContext';

export function useCanvas() {
  const { state, dispatch } = useFloorPlan();
  const isDragging = useRef(false);
  const dragStart = useRef({ x: 0, y: 0 });
  
  const handleWheel = useCallback((e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const delta = e.deltaY > 0 ? 0.9 : 1.1;
    const newZoom = Math.max(0.5, Math.min(3, state.viewState.zoom * delta));
    
    dispatch({
      type: 'SET_VIEW_STATE',
      payload: { zoom: newZoom }
    });
  }, [state.viewState.zoom, dispatch]);
  
  const handleMouseDown = useCallback((e) => {
    if (e.button === 1) { // ì¤‘ê°„ ë²„íŠ¼ìœ¼ë¡œ íŒ¬
      isDragging.current = true;
      dragStart.current = { x: e.clientX, y: e.clientY };
    }
  }, []);
  
  // ... ë” ë§ì€ ì´ë²¤íŠ¸ í•¸ë“¤ëŸ¬
  
  return {
    handleWheel,
    handleMouseDown,
    // ...
  };
}
ğŸ“‹ Phase 5: ëª¨ë‹¬ ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ ë§ˆì´ê·¸ë ˆì´ì…˜
5.1 BaseModal ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸

// components/Modals/BaseModal.jsx
import { X } from 'lucide-react';

export default function BaseModal({ isOpen, onClose, title, children }) {
  if (!isOpen) return null;
  
  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center">
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-50" onClick={onClose} />
      <div className="relative bg-white rounded-lg shadow-xl max-w-md w-full">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-4 border-b">
          <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold">{title}</h3>
          <button onClick={onClose} className="p-1 hover:bg-gray-100 rounded">
            <X size={20} />
          </button>
        </div>
        <div className="p-4">{children}</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

const handleResizeRoom = (room) => {
  const currentRoom = rooms.find(r => r.id === room.id);
  if (currentRoom) {
    setSelectedRoom(currentRoom);
    setShowDimensionEdit(true);  // ëª¨ë‹¬ í‘œì‹œ
    setShowContextMenu(false);
  }
};

javascript
const handleDimensionApply = (roomId, newDimensions) => {
  setRooms(prevRooms => prevRooms.map(room => {
    if (room.id === roomId) {
      return { ...room, ...newDimensions };  // ìƒˆë¡œìš´ ì¹˜ìˆ˜ë¡œ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸
    }
    return room;
  }));

// íšŒì „ í›„ ê·¸ë¦¬ë“œ ì •ë ¬ì„ ìœ„í•œ ì˜¤í”„ì…‹ ê³„ì‚°
if (angle % (Math.PI / 2) === 0) { // 90ë„ì˜ ë°°ìˆ˜ì¼ ë•Œ
  // ì‹¤ì˜ ì¤‘ì‹¬ì—ì„œ ì™¼ìª½ ìœ„ ëª¨ì„œë¦¬ê¹Œì§€ì˜ ê±°ë¦¬
  const halfWidth = room.width / 2;
  const halfHeight = room.height / 2;
  
  // í˜„ì¬ ì™¼ìª½ ìœ„ ëª¨ì„œë¦¬ ìœ„ì¹˜
  const cornerX = room.x - halfWidth;
  const cornerY = room.y - halfHeight;
  
  // ê·¸ë¦¬ë“œì— ë§ì¶”ê¸° ìœ„í•œ ì˜¤í”„ì…‹ ê³„ì‚° (0.5 ë‹¨ìœ„)
  const gridSize = 0.5 * SCALE_FACTOR; // 5 pixels
  const offsetX = cornerX % gridSize;
  const offsetY = cornerY % gridSize;
  
  // ê°€ì¥ ê°€ê¹Œìš´ ê·¸ë¦¬ë“œ êµì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì´ë™
  if (offsetX !== 0) {
    room.x += (offsetX > gridSize/2) ? (gridSize - offsetX) : -offsetX;
  }
  if (offsetY !== 0) {
    room.y += (offsetY > gridSize/2) ? (gridSize - offsetY) : -offsetY;
  }
}

  ? state.rooms.filter(r => r.floor !== 'B1')
  : state.rooms.filter(r => r.floor === floor);
